Additionally handles IPv6 addresses.\\n313: \\n314:     QUrl.fromUserInput handles something like '::1' as a file URL instead of an\\n315:     IPv6, so we first try to handle it as a valid IPv6, and if that fails we\\n316:     use QUrl.fromUserInput.\\n317: \\n318:     WORKAROUND - https://bugreports.qt.io/browse/QTBUG-41089\\n319:     FIXME - Maybe https://codereview.qt-project.org/#/c/93851/ has a better way\\n320:             to solve this?\\n321:     https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/109\\n322: \\n323:     Args:\\n324:         urlstr: The URL as string.\\n325: \\n326:     Return:\\n327:         The converted QUrl.\\n328:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n329:     # First we try very liberally to separate something like an IPv6 from the\\n330:     # rest (e.g. path info or The function `incdec_number` is at line 583. Let me analyze it:\n\nThe problem is in the regex and how the URL segments are processed:\n\n1. **Lines 562-579**: The URL segments are extracted using `QUrl.PrettyDecoded` mode. This partially decodes the URL, but the issue is that when it's \"pretty decoded\", some percent-encoded characters are being decoded back to their original form.\n\n2. **Line 618**: The regex pattern is:\n```python\nmatch = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\\\\d+)(.*)', getter(url))\n```\n\nThis tries to avoid matching numbers that are preceded by `%` or `%.`, but:\n- If a URL contains `%3A5`, and the getter returns it as `:5` (because PrettyDecoded decodes `%3A` to `:`), then the regex will match the `5` in `%3A5` and try to modify it.\n- Even worse, the setter will then reconstruct the string without the percent encoding!\n\n3. **Lines 537-541**: The decrement logic doesn't properly check if the result would be negative before the decrement. It only checks `if val < count`, which means:\n   - If `val = 1` and `count = 2`, then `val < count` is True, so it raises an error\n   - But the condition should properly handle this\n\nWait, looking more carefully at line 538:\n```python\nif val < count:\n    raise IncDecError(\"Can't decrement {} by {}!\".format(val, count), url)\n```\n\nActually, this SHOULD prevent negative values! If val=1 and count=2, then `1 < 2` is True, so it should raise an error. But the issue description says negative values are allowed...\n\nLet me re-read the regex more carefully. The regex is:\n\n\n- `(.*\\D|^)` - Capture everything up to the last non-digit or start\n- `(?<!%)(?<!%)` - Negative lookbehind: not preceded by `%` or `%.`\n- `(0*)` - Capture leading zeros\n- `(\\\\d+)` - Capture the number\n- `(.*)` - Capture rest\n\nThe core issue is that when the URL is \"pretty decoded\" (e.g., `%3A5` becomes `:5`), the negative lookbehind fails to prevent matching the number, since the `%` is no longer there. The regex then captures and modifies the digit, and the setter reconstructs it without proper percent-encoding.","signature":"EuoSCkYICxgCKkDk0UlbJJGFSsL/woOTIAFboVGpVh3iwxdxTF7pqleCpemEMZO5HdyG0OOSDbSNUXijRjKmGKubtQc0ifhA6zibEgxDbtkh9U7F32FiP6EaDMpYZAMqPZoFf38btyIw380rywPNLarQHErGaqLX44A49wkyWrDNJ910BQKiZBefIyGRcFx5ncDR3Yzez3irKtER7tZqy3k8rOHwaz70RO6QfFIEJmnStvxCj3Cg7oxW7yNN0go55kCNl3X7Hvf/u6eFD2j4A2z6+K6TRFEyUJ8qTb4jLq5r7DRF0T7SD3t740k5b9F8/dc9rqp4kQcAqAdPeQ/dqhPP1kDh4x95dVbTBZIVwCQ6874dtmaDuLY2YaPdWdijse2SvYyXLAhVMWtGu8RILxV3k0KAImGYV47Ru0LpBe+BGYdg2GF2kgnmg5gecaVg2l6YnKtCnI66I4wrVuHOfRDndXF7yhhiP7zgLw/3WdOxjTmcMDIy/PXnAIJujvn/pkQeJ+CoyINyv5LeXKYtLFDCkJpfgCQ1V14sRzF0kYsNQa29LGYxbYbgApnxPwDpE2a1eiBT5p/kgjWnCD44nyVTLY65ipcr6zxPWdurja2FJx9v7npI3avB3YNjhwGXeIxgy6/1mKfHR3kudfP82JLlEN9Lhlc3ZZxJ/0KwOMbbCYiV0SjWBpE70xWSiS9YBr2+1J43b8YGmYXEA/DDuTTtGDby8Feji/rIM/OFX0sPtWTSMBdln4fSC5NSJTt1gVNmC8JfOeAP/z/30jq651aE4oOH1j3N5ouFAUx7iVhiU07CF//AkuLAzqAFOFOymD0gY5iTmfzSE4mL3Nk66z4EU8+KwDb8j7xBp6rIM0ErHP5Cxx8by4JWfdhGRuRIZDkmRqV+01YQi1a+xwfoRd3yyX9y0YjfgGMhPf2DA2zpEDZ1pkxzpeZlQ73RTeDVsYkLJ+cPtogOq4gAg1GmaKaCOBoAxMjJsCy47xSBuk0unwlmHo7AOCZL4bE2IiTzbdgaK9CHq1tNOAInLer5w0Byeq8Kobd1wo7PXGLKznjATNe2aztWPFAJGKAqVOBmC6xu3oy6jdIy9TWsUIVMIbROFLygjLBUuaD2omqTBuHvX8yNVvVjRAnN09EwEvV5M9UWNAmA6Gjt8f/rFDJeZ1TqMW9VH1XP01pRum8sjHsJ5Wxwryv/qGPwI2rdsw30jW7QAuSsZuaN/S7HWxjPMGMgrhdoNtKNz7LwJ6bAyPEnhHm5iNcCz2P3c/UrwewTAxU9Y/s/oA7RmvmPmYhoMuVxq4Br6u1ON7RS0TyZdxdvqX+oz23uL8a2Vkvw64rzMuJ91PYLc6rtF5aSeQQsJ9EE8lTdlcETGvTiLMrg3sVZTCmgs5urC1FW0zNK59CD6yinDGgSywiwXmW0FBEKZ8BAXTya1Ibs8zmaeRvpaYGFJU2Pv4vbLX/2NqvILFyOTWxa67Txdc6QsQ7kTf72jIksFmCNd12lRC/LCj+GsUO1Kh7vpqzJSGUaHEHAsPqnF6xAwt54eTsT5N9qTRXeI9461A1v/nHNEV8estR3dPUiRjN5nUJ7HmcPfoizQAKiom3Gc5MPvUib64Rx4ccXBM8tqe4gbMEvyi+5FzZGfX5UWa7lU11vJtnvFfQhn6lfUSu7JnZVwWyvlGtf9sfl7duuvCkqtheq4deAAW4fTu9fqE/kUsejnlALNdTsZXY302uFGfD6LjG1jdAqWKBKJ4YxefSOY1R2zRKB1t94OKEVt6jbbqVAdGbF1g7D92r/ltaTSY1RYWQrfHm0JJD2hhpH1fxEkRK4SpAPfYBHIcU14GD3gTpRNXCQ0n5aARVmmKTN8pOKaQoIBfLhcue+ZUhar39S7t4y0wqsBZJhiFa2ChDkLvbS0VSX46s1NrxxnNcvbPqp4v5OihM1jI+yR99iadXozsnnW9FNZ7llWg9DCR9Y domain\"\n    is. All further domains are ignored.\n\n    For example example.com and www.example.com are considered the same. but\n    example.co.uk and test.co.uk are not.\n\n    Return:\n        True if the domains are the same, False otherwise.\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\n    if not url1.isValid():\n        raise InvalidUrlError(url1)\n    if not url2.isValid():\n        raise InvalidUrlError(url2)\n\n    suffix1 = url1.topLevelDomain()\n    suffix2 = url2.topLevelDomain()\n    if suffix1 == '':\n        return url1.host() == url2.host()\n\n    if suffix1 != suffix2:\n        return False\n\n    domain1 = url1.host()[:-len(suffix1)].split('.')[-1]\n    domain2 = url2.host()[:-len(suffix2)].split('.')[-1]\n    return domain1 == domain2\n\n\ndef encoded_url(url):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Return the fully encoded url as string.\n\n    Args:\n        url: The url to encode as QUrl.\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\n    return bytes(url.toEncoded()).decode('ascii')\n\n\nclass IncDecError(Exception):\n\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Exception raised by incdec_number on problems.\n\n    Attributes:\n        msg: The error message.\n        url: The QUrl which caused the error.\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\n\n    def __init__(self, msg, url):\n        super().__init__(msg)\n        self.url = url\n        self.msg = msg\n\n    def __str__(self):\n        return '{}: {}'.format(self.msg, self.url.toString())\n\n\ndef _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Get an incremented/decremented URL based on a URL match.\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    pre, zeroes, number, post = match.groups()\n    # This should always succeed because we match \\\\d+\n    val = int(number)\n    if incdec == 'decrement':\n        if val < count:\n            raise IncDecError(\"Can't decrement {} by {}!\".format(val, count),\n                              url)\n        val -= count\n    elif incdec == 'increment':\n        val += count\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(\"Invalid value {} for incdec!\".format(incdec))\n    if zeroes:\n        if len(number) < len(str(val)):\n            zeroes = zeroes[1:]\n        elif len(number) > len(str(val)):\n            zeroes += '0'\n\n    return ''.join([pre, zeroes, str(val), post])\n\n\n# Order of the segments in a URL.\n# Each list entry is a tuple of (path name (string), getter, setter).\n# Note that the getters must not use FullyDecoded decoded mode to prevent loss\n# of information. (host and path use FullyDecoded by default)\n_URL_SEGMENTS = [\n    (\n        'host',\n        lambda url: url.host(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, host: url.setHost(host, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'port',\n        lambda url: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',\n        lambda url, x: url.setPort(int(x))),\n    (\n        'path',\n        lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, path: url.setPath(path, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'query',\n        lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, query: url.setQuery(query, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'anchor',\n        lambda url: url.fragment(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, fragment: url.setFragment(fragment, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n]\n\n\ndef incdec_number(url, incdec, count=1, segments=None):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Find a number in the url and increment or decrement it.\n\n    Args:\n        url: The current url\n        incdec: Either 'increment' or 'decrement'\n        count: The number to increment or decrement by\n        segments: A set of URL segments to search. Valid segments are:\n                  'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'.\n                  Default: {'path', 'query'}\n\n    Return:\n        The new url with the number incremented/decremented.\n\n    Raises IncDecError if the url contains no number.\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\n    if not url.isValid():\n        raise InvalidUrlError(url)\n\n    if segments is None:\n        segments = {'path', 'query'}\n    valid_segments = {'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'}\n    if segments - valid_segments:\n        extra_elements = segments - valid_segments\n        raise IncDecError(\"Invalid segments: {}\".format(\n            ', '.join(extra_elements)), url)\n\n    # Make a copy of the QUrl so we don't modify the original\n    url = QUrl(url)\n    # We're searching the last number so we walk the url segments backwards\n    for segment, getter, setter in reversed(_URL_SEGMENTS):\n        if segment not in segments:\n            continue\n\n        # This should always succeed because we match \\d+\n    val = int(number)\n    if incdec == 'decrement':\n        if val < count:\n            raise IncDecError(\"Can't decrement {} by {}!\".format(val, count),\n                              url)\n        val -= count\n    elif incdec == 'increment':\n        val += count\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(\"Invalid value {} for incdec!\".format(incdec))\n    if zeroes:\n        if len(number) < len(str(val)):\n            zeroes = zeroes[1:]\n        elif len(number) > len(str(val)):\n            zeroes += '0'\n\n    return ''.join([pre, zeroes, str(val), post])\n\n\n# Order of the segments in a URL.\n# Each list entry is a tuple of (path name (string), getter, setter).\n# Note that the getters must not use FullyDecoded decoded mode to prevent loss\n# of information. (host and path use FullyDecoded by default)\n_URL_SEGMENTS = [\n    (\n        'host',\n        lambda url: url.host(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, host: url.setHost(host, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'port',\n        lambda url: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',\n        lambda url, x: url.setPort(int(x))),\n    (\n        'path',\n        lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, path: url.setPath(path, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'query',\n        lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, query: url.setQuery(query, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'anchor',\n        lambda url: url.fragment(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, fragment: url.setFragment(fragment, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n]\n\n\ndef incdec_number(url, incdec, count=1, segments=None):\n    \"\"\"Find a number in the url and increment or decrement it.\n\n    Args:\n        url: The current url\n        incdec: Either 'increment' or 'decrement'\n        count: The number to increment or decrement by\n        segments: A set of URL segments to search. Valid segments are:\n                  'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'.\n                  Default: {'path', 'query'}\n\n    Return:\n        The new url with the number incremented/decremented.\n\n    Raises IncDecError if the url contains no number.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not url.isValid():\n        raise InvalidUrlError(url)\n\n    if segments is None:\n        segments = {'path', 'query'}\n    valid_segments = {'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'}\n    if segments - valid_segments:\n        extra_elements = segments - valid_segments\n        raise IncDecError(\"Invalid segments: {}\".format(\n            ', '.join(extra_elements)), url)\n\n    # Make a copy of the QUrl so we don't modify the original\n    url = QUrl(url)\n    # We're searching the last number so we walk the url segments backwards\n    for segment, getter, setter in reversed(_URL_SEGMENTS):\n        if segment not in segments:\n            continue\n\n        # Get the last number in a string not preceded by regex '%' or '%.'.\n        match = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)',\n                             getter(url))\n        if not match:\n            continue\n\n        setter(url, _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count))\n        return url\n\n    raise IncDecError(\"No number found in URL!\", url)\n\n\ndef file_url(path):\n    \"\"\"Return a file:// url (as string) to the given local path.\n\n    Arguments:\n        path: The absolute path to the local file\n    \"\"\"\n    return QUrl.fromLocalFile(path).toString(QUrl.FullyEncoded)\n\n\ndef data_url(mimetype, data):\n    \"\"\"Get a data: QUrl for the given data.\"\"\"\n    b64 = base64.b64encode(data).decode('ascii')\n    url = QUrl('data:{};base64,{}'.format(mimetype, b64))\n    qtutils.ensure_valid(url)\n    return url\n\n\ndef safe_display_string(qurl):\n    \"\"\"Get a IDN-homograph phishing safe form of the given QUrl.\n\n    If we're dealing with a Punycode-encoded URL, this prepends the hostname in\n    its encoded form, to make sure those URLs are distinguishable.\n\n    See https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/2547\n    and https://bugreports.qt.io/browse/QTBUG-60365\n    \"\"\"\n    if not qurl.isValid():\n        raise InvalidUrlError(qurl)\n\n    host = qurl.host(QUrl.FullyEncoded)\n    if '..' in host:  # _parse_search_term(s):\n    \"\"\"Get a search engine name and search term from a string.\n\n    Args:\n        s: The string to get a search engine for.\n\n    Return:\n        A (engine, term) tuple, where engine is None for the default engine.\n    \"\"\"\n    s = s.strip()\n    split = s.split(maxsplit=1)\n\n    if len(split) == 2:\n        engine = split[0]\n        try:\n Additionally handles IPv6 addresses.\n\n    QUrl.fromUserInput handles something like '::1' as a file URL instead of an\n    IPv6, so we first try to handle it as a valid IPv6, and if that fails we\n \"\"\"\n    url_error = url.errorString()\n    if url_error:\n        return base + \" - {}\".format(url_error)\n    else:\n        return base\n\n\ndef same_domain(url1, url2):\n    \"\"\"Check if url1 and url2 belong to the same website.\n\n    This will use a \"public suffix list\" to determine what a \"top level domain\"\n    is. All further domains are ignored.\n\n    For example example.com and www.example.com are considered the same. but\n    example.co.uk and test.co.uk are not.\n\n    Return:\n        True if the domains are the same, False otherwise.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not url1.isValid():\n        raise InvalidUrlError(url1)\n    if not url2.isValid():\n        raise InvalidUrlError(url2)\n\n    suffix1 = url1.topLevelDomain()\n    suffix2 = url2.topLevelDomain()\n    if suffix1 == '':\n        return url1.host() == url2.host()\n\n    if suffix1 != suffix2:\n        return False\n\n    domain1 = url1.host()[:-len(suffix1)].split('.')[-1]\n    domain2 = url2.host()[:-len(suffix2)].split('.')[-1]\n    return domain1 == domain2\n\n\ndef encoded_url(url):\n    \"\"\"Return the fully encoded url as string.\n\n    Args:\n        url: The url to encode as QUrl.\n    \"\"\"\n    return bytes(url.toEncoded()).decode('ascii')\n\n\nclass IncDecError(Exception):\n\n    \"\"\"Exception raised by incdec_number on problems.\n\n    Attributes:\n        msg: The error message.\n        url: The QUrl which caused the error.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, msg, url):\n        super().__init__(msg)\n        self.url = url\n        self.msg = msg\n\n    def __str__(self):\n        return '{}: {}'.format(self.msg, self.url.toString())\n\n\ndef _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count):\n    \"\"\"Get an incremented/decremented URL based on a URL match.\"\"\"\n    pre, zeroes, number, post = match.groups()\n    # This should always succeed because we match \\d+\n    val = int(number)\n    if incdec == 'decrement':\n        if val < count:\n            raise IncDecError(\"Can't decrement {} by {}!\".format(val, count),\n                              url)\n        val -= count\n    elif incdec == 'increment':\n        val += count\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(\"Invalid value {} for incdec!\".format(incdec))\n    if zeroes:\n        if len(number) < len(str(val)):\n            zeroes = zeroes[1:]\n        elif len(number) > len(str(val)):\n            zeroes += '0'\n\n    return ''.join([pre, zeroes, str(val), post])\n\n\n# Order of the segments in a URL.\n# Each list entry is a tuple of (path name (string), getter, setter).\n# Note that the getters must not use FullyDecoded decoded mode to prevent loss\n# of information. (host and path use FullyDecoded by default)\n_URL_SEGMENTS = [\n    (\n        'host',\n        lambda url: url.host(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, host: url.setHost(host, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'port',\n        lambda url: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',\n        lambda url, x: url.setPort(int(x))),\n    (\n        'path',\n        lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, path: url.setPath(path, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'query',\n        lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, query: url.setQuery(query, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'anchor',\n        lambda url: url.fragment(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, fragment: url.setFragment(fragment, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n]\n\n\ndef incdec_number(url, incdec, count=1, segments=None):\n    \"\"\"Find a number in the url and increment or decrement it.\n\n    Args:\n        url: The current url\n        incdec: Either 'increment' or 'decrement'\n        count: The number to increment or decrement by\n        segments: A set of URL segments to search. Valid segments are:\n                  'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'.\n                  Default: {'path', 'query'}\n\n    Return:\n        The new url with the number incremented/decremented.\n\n    Raises IncDecError if the url contains no number.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not url.isValid():\n        raise InvalidUrlError(url)\n\n    if segments is None:\n        segments = {'path', 'query'}\n    valid_segments = {'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'}\n    if segments - valid_segments:\n        extra_elements = segments - valid_segments\n        raise IncDecError(\"Invalid segments: {}\".format(\n            ', '.join(extra_elements)), url)\n\n    # Make a copy of the QUrl so we don't modify the original\n    url = QUrl(url)\n    # We're searching the last number so we walk the url segments backwards\n    for segment, getter, setter in reversed(_URL_SEGMENTS):\n        if segment not in segments:\n            continue\n\n        #
